5. Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na muhu dɛ hɔn bo etutu yi? Wɔadan hɔn ekyir; wɔabɔ hɔn akatakyi no egu, na woeguan ntsɛntsɛm. Wommbu hɔn kɔn ekyir: hu wɔ mbea nyina, EWURADZE na ɔse.
6. Ɔhoɔharfo nntum nnguan nnkɔ, eso ɔkatakyi mmfi nsa; kwaamu afamu esutsen Eufrates ho na woefintsiw na wɔahwehwe ase.
7. Woana na ɔasoɛr noho yi dɛ Nael a n'esu bu asorɛkye begyabegya dɛ nsutsen yi?
8. Egypt asoɛr dɛ Nael, dɛ nsutsen a n'esu rubu asorɛkye begyabegya: na ɔse, Mibeyir, mebɛkata asaase no do; mebɛsɛɛ kurow no na no mu mba no.
9. Mpɔnkɔ e, hom mbɔ mfa mu; na ntseaseanam e, hom mbɔ kyirdidi! Hom mma akatakyi mfir edzi: Kus na Put a wokurakura kyɛm; na Ludfo a wokurakura egyen, na wɔkontokontom no.
10. Na da no yɛ EWURADZE, dɔm EWURADZE, ne da, awerdzi da a, ama oeedzi n'atamfo wer: na afona bedzidzi amee, na ɔanom hɔn bɔgyaa ɔabow: na EWURADZE, dɔm EWURADZE, wɔ okum afɔr bi wɔ kwaa mu asaase do wɔ esutsen Eufrates ho.
11. Egypt ne babaa ɔbaabun e, fow kɔ Gilead kɛgye edur! Eyɛ edur pii kwa; ɔyarsa biara nnyi hɔ ma wo.
12. Amanaman atse w'enyimguase, na wo nkekamu ahyɛ asaase ma tɔ: na ɔkatakyi asoasoa ɔkatakyi do, hɔn beenu no abɔ mu ahwe ase.
13. Asɛm a EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia, mbrɛ Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar bɛba abɔbɔ Egypt asaase no.
14. Hom mpaa mu nka no Egypt, na hom mfa ntahye Migidɔl, hom ntahye no Nof na Tapanhes: hom nka dɛ, Gyina kan, na siesie woho; na afona no bedzidzi etwa wo ho ehyia.
15. Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na w'ahoɔdzenfo wɔapra hɔn kɔ yi? Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na w'anantwi enngyina? Osiandɛ EWURADZE paam hɔn kɔree.
16. Ɔmaa pii fintsifintsiwii, nyew, wɔhwehwee ase dedaa hɔnho do: na wɔsee dɛ, Hom nsoɛr ma yɛnsan nkɔ hɛn nkorɔfo, na hɛn awobea no do hɔ, mfi afona a ɔrehyɛ hɛn no ano.
17. Wɔkekaa mu wɔ hɔ dɛ, Egypthen Farao yɛ dede ara kwa; ɔama hyɛber no etwa mu asen.
18. Metse ase yi, Ɔhen a ne dzin dze dɔm EWURADZE no na ɔse, ampaara mbrɛ Tabor tse wɔ mbepɔw mu, na mbrɛ Karmel tse wɔ po ho no, dɛmara na no so bɛba.
19. Ɔwo babaa a etse Egypt, siesie woho kɔ ndɔmmum mu: na Nof bɛdan amamfo, na wɔahyew a, obi renntsena do bio.
20. Egypt yɛ ɔnantwiber a no ho yɛ fɛw; na ɔsɛɛ fi kwaamu afamu aba no do.
21. N'apaafo so a wɔtse no mu no, wɔtse dɛ nantwibuw mu anantwimba; na hɔn so wɔadandan hɔnho na wɔabɔ mu eguanguan, woenngyina: osiandɛ hɔn mbusu da, hɔn sera ber no, aba hɔn do.
22. Ne ndze bɛgyegye dɛ ɔwɔ dze; osiandɛ n'atamfo nam reba, na wɔdze nkuma aba no do, dɛ nduatowfo.
23. Wobobu no kwaa, EWURADZE na ɔse, naaso worunntum nnhwehwɛ mu; osiandɛ wɔdɔɔ so sen mbɛbɛw, na wɔkan hɔn dodow a ɔnnyɛ.
24. Wɔbɛma Egypt babaa n'enyi ato; wobeyi no ahyɛ kwaa mu ɔman no nsa.
25. Dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no, ɔse dɛ: Hwɛ mebɛtsea Amon a ɔwɔ No, na Farao, na Egypt ɔnye n'abosom, na n'ahemfo; mekyerɛ Farao na hɔn a wɔtwer no no:
26. na mibeyi hɔn mahyɛ hɔn a wɔhwehwɛ hɔn nkwa no nsa, na Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar nsa, na n'akowaa nsa: na n'ekyir no wɔbɛtsena do dɛ tsetse nda no, EWURADZE na ɔse.
27. Na ɔwo m'akowaa Jakob, mma nnsuro, na Israel so, mma wo bo nntu: na, hwɛ, mebɛgye wo nkwa mefi ekyirekyir, na w'asefo efi ndɔmmum asaase do: na Jakob bɛsan, na ɔbɛtsena ase dwudwoodwo, na obiara remma onnsuro.
28. M'akowaa Jakob, mma nnsuro, EWURADZE na ɔse; na mowɔ wo nkyɛn: na mebɛma amanaman a mabɔ hɔn apetse do no woewie sa, naaso ɔwo dze, meremma innwie sa; na mbom mebɛtsea wo dɛ mbrɛ ɔfata, na meremma emmfa woho tɔtrɔtɔ ara da.

## Tsir 47

1. EWURADZE asɛm a ɔbaa nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia hɔ wɔ Filistiafo ho ansaana Farao robɔ Gaza.
2. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Hwɛ, esu rema noho do efi kwaamu afamu, na ɔabɛyɛ ɔwora a oeyir, na ɔaseram asaase no na dza ɔwɔ mu nyina do, kurow no na hɔn a wɔtse mu do: na nyimpa bɛkeka mu, na hɔn a wɔtse asaase no do no nyina abɔ mbubuw.
3. Na mpɔnkɔ hɔn ntɔtse a osisi famu pipi no ne gyegye, ne ntseaseanam ne nkyirdidi, no nhwiir no kurduduyɛ ntsi, egyanom nndan hɔn enyi nnhwɛ hɔn mba wɔ hɔn nsa a agow ntsi;
4. osian da a ɔreba no ntsi, ɔreba abɛsɛɛ Filistiafo nyina, ebotwitwa Taere na Sidon ɔboafo a ɔaka biara efi hɔ: osiandɛ EWURADZE resɛɛ Filistiafo, Kaftor nsupruw mu hɔn a wɔaka no.
5. Etsipaa aba Gaza do; Ashkelon ataa dzinn na hɔn bɔnsa mu nkaa no asɛɛ pasaa: ebɔtotow woho akam ekesi dabɛn?
6. Ao, EWURADZE n'afona! Onkodu dabɛn ara na ayɛ komm? Fa woho kɛhyɛ wo bɔha mu; gye w'ahom, na taa dzinn.
7. Ibesi dɛn ayɛ komm, ber a EWURADZE dze asodzi bi ahyɛ wo nsa yi? Ashkelon, na mpoano hɔ na ɔahyɛ dɛ ɔmbra.

## Tsir 48

1. Moab dze, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no se nye yi: Nebo ndue, osiandɛ wɔabɔ no! Woegu Kiriataim n'enyim ase, wɔagye: woegu aban dzendzen no n'enyim ase na wɔadwerew no.
2. Nkamfo nnyi hɔ bio mma Moab; woetu no ho egyina bɔn wɔ Hesbon dɛ, Hom mbra, ma yentwa no nkyen mma ɔaannyɛ ɔman bio. Madmen, ɔwo so wɔbɛma ayɛ foo; afona betsiw wo.
3. Nkekamu ndze fi Horonaim, afofa na ɔsɛɛ kɛse!
4. Wɔasɛɛ Moab; no nkɔkowaba rekeka mu.
5. Na Luhit afowee na wɔdze osu araa bɔfow akɔ sor; na Horonaim esianee na wɔatse ɔsɛɛ ne nkekamu ho mbubuwbɔ.
6. Hom nguanguan, hom ngye hom akra nkwa, na hom nyɛ dɛ sar do asoaso.
7. Na osiandɛ ɔwo atwer wo ndwuma na w'akoradze ntsi, wo so wɔbɛfa wo: na Kemos bɔkɔ ndɔmmum, n'asɔfoe na n'asafohen ka ho.
8. Na afofanyi no bɛba kurow biara do, na kurow biara rimmfi nsa; bɔnsa so bɛhera, na asaase taae asɛɛ; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE aka no.
9. Hom mma Moab nkaadum, na ɔsɛɛ ara na wɔbɛsɛɛ no: no nkurow bɛyɛ amamfo, na obiara nnkɛtsena mu.
10. Ndom nka nyia ɔyɛ EWURADZE n'edwuma akwadwer mu, na ndom nka nyia osianka n'afona fi bɔgya mu.
11. Moab atsena ase ahodwe mu fi ne mbofraber mu, na ɔagyen ataa n'ase dɛ wenyin, na wonnhuee no mmfii adze kor mu nnkɔr adze kor mu, eso ɔnnkɔr ndɔmmum da: dɛm ntsi na ne dɛw aka no mu, na no huam so nnsakyeree.
12. Dɛm ntsi, hwɛ, nda reba a, EWURADZE na ɔse, mobɔsoma hɔn a wohue gu ma wɔaaba no do, ma woeehue no egu, na wɔaabobɔ hɔn mbɔdambɔ no.
13. Na Moab n'enyi bɔto Kemos ho, dɛ mbrɛ Israel fifo hɔn enyi too hɔn awerɛhyɛmu Bɛtɛl ho no.
14. Ɔyɛ dɛn na hom se dɛ, Yɛyɛ akatakyi na akofo a yebotum ɔko no?
15. Nyia ɔbɔɔ Moab na no nkurow no afow kɔ mu, na ne mberantsɛ a wɔasan mu eyi hɔn no esian kɔ ekumii, ɔhen a ne dzin dze dɔm EWURADZE no na ɔse.
16. Moab no mbusu abɛn reba, na n'amandzehu reba ntsɛntsɛm.
17. Hom a hom abɔ no ho aprɔw nyina, hom ngyam no, na hom a hom nyim ne dzin nyina; hom nse dɛ, Nhwɛ, mbrɛ poma a ɔyɛ dzen, na enyimnyam abaa no, edua ebu a!
18. Ɔwo babaa a etse Dibon, fi w'enyimnyam mu sian, na tsena nsukɔm mu, na nyia ɔfa Moab afo no aba wo do, ɔasɛɛ w'aban dzendzen no.
19. Hom a hom tse Aroer e, kegyina akwan nkyɛn, na tsɛw: bisa nyia oruguan, na nyia oefi nsa no; se dɛ, Wɔyɛ no dɛn?
20. Woegu Moab n'enyim ase; osiandɛ woedwuruw no egu famu: hom mbɔ mbubuw na hom nkekamu; hom nka wɔ Arnon dɛ, Moab abɔ.
21. Na atsɛmbu aba asaase taae no do; ɔaba Holon, Jahza, Mefaat;
22. Dibon, Nebo, Bɛt-diblathaim;
23. Kiriataim, Bɛt-gamul, Bɛt-meon;
24. Keriot, na Bozra, na Moab asaase do nkorɔfo a wɔwɔ ekyirekyir, na dza wɔbɛn nyina do.
25. Woetwa Moab n'ambɛn, na woebu n'abasa, EWURADZE na ɔse.
26. Hom mma ɔmbow nsa; osiandɛ okunkoon noho wɔ EWURADZE do: na Moab bɛyankayankam ne fe mu, na ɔno so wɔdze no esi atwetwe.
27. Na aso Israel annyɛ atwetwe amma wo? Aso wohun no ewifo mu? Na ɔwo eka no ho asɛm ara apem a, ewosow wo tsir.
28. Ao Moab mba e, hom ndan nkurow no ngya, na hom ntsena abotan do. Hom nyɛ dɛ ebubur a ɔyɛ no buw wɔ itu no ano no.
29. Yɛatse Moab n'ahokyerɛ, dɛ ɔkyerɛ no ho dodow; n'ahomemado, na no nkontompɔ, na n'ahopɔw, na n'akoma ne ntsɛn.
30. Minyim n'enyiansɔ, EWURADZE na ɔse, dɛ ne nyinara gyan; n'ahohyehyɛ enntum hwee yɛ.
31. Dɛm ntsi nna mobɔ Moab ho mbubuw; nyew, mebɛkeka mu wɔ Moab nyina ho: na Kir-heres mbarimba ntsi wobedzi nkɔmbɔ.
32. Ao Sibma wenyindua, medze dza ɔkyɛn Jazer no su na mubosu wo: w'abaw atra po ekodu Jazer po ho mpo: wo hyewber nduadzewa na wo wenyin nduadzewa do na ɔsɛɛfo no ebotu ahyɛ.
33. Na woeyi enyigye na dɛw efi mfuwa prɔmprɔm na Moab asaase no do; na mama wenyin asa wɔ wenyinntwer no mu: obiara mmfa esebɔ ntsiatsia do; esebɔ no rennyɛ enyigye esebɔ bi.
34. Ofi Hesbon nkekamu no do dze kesi Eleale mpo, dze kesi Jahaz mpo, na wɔama hɔn ndze do, ofi Zoar dze kesi Horonaim mpo, dze kesi Eglath-selisiya: na Nimrim esuesu bɛdan asaase kɛsɛɛ.
35. Bio so mebɛma nyia ɔbɔ afɔr wɔ no mu sorɔnsorɔmbea, na nyia ɔhyew nduhuam ma n'abosom no abɔ adze wɔ Moab.
36. Dɛm ntsi m'akoma gyegye ma Moab dɛ atɛntɛbɛn, na m'akoma gyegye dɛ atɛntɛbɛn ma Kir-heres mbarimba: dɛm ntsi adze pii a woenya no ahera.
37. Ne tsir nyina apepa, na n'abɔdwesa nyina ekukuw: nsa nyina ho ayɛ akam akam, na eyitam sisi asen.
38. Moab adan nyina etsifi na n'abrɔn do sukwadwom wɔ mbea nyina: na mabɔ Moab dɛ senaba a enyigye nnyi mu, EWURADZE na ɔse.
39. Mbrɛ woesi edwuruw no a! Mbrɛ wodua bɔ mbubuw a! Mbrɛ Moab edua dze enyito adan n'ekyir a! Dɛm na Moab bɛyɛ atwetwesi na akomatu ama hɔn a wɔabɔ no ho aprɔw nyina.
40. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Hwɛ, obotu dɛ ɔkɔr, na ɔatserɛw ne ntsaban mu aba Moab do.
41. Keriot wɔagye, na wɔakɔ n'akoban no ntuae. Da no mu, Moab mbarimba akatakyi hɔn akoma bɛyɛ dɛ ɔbaa a ɔroko awoo n'akoma.
42. Na wɔbɛsɛɛ Moab ma ɔrennyɛ ɔman bio, osiandɛ oekunkon noho wɔ EWURADZE do.
43. Moab mba e, suro, na mona, na efir, aba wo do, EWURADZE na ɔse.
44. Nyia obefi suro enyim eguan no ɔbɔkɔtɔ mona no mu; na nyia ɔbɔfow efi mona no mu no, efir no bɛpa no: osiandɛ medze asotwe bɛba ɔno noara Moab no do, EWURADZE na ɔse.
45. Hɔn a woguanee a wonnyi ahoɔdzen no gyinagyina Hesbon nwinwin ase: na gya fir Hesbon efir edzi, na gyaframee fi Sihon ne finimfin, na ɔahyew Moab no kutuwdo, na weɔɔweɔɔyɛfo no hɔn etsifi pampamu.
46. Moab, due! Kemos man abɔ: na wɔafa wo mbabanyin no ndɔmmum, na wɔdze wo mbabaa kɔ ndɔmmumkɔ.
47. Naaso medze Moab befi ndɔmmum asan aba wɔ nda a odzi ekyir no mu, EWURADZE na ɔse. Iyi nye Moab do atsɛmbu.

## Tsir 49

1. Dza ɔfa Ammonmba ho. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Aso Israel nnyi mbabanyin? Aso onnyi owuodzi? Afei ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na Malkam enya Gad, na no nkorɔfo tsenatsena no nkurow mu yi?
2. Dɛm ntsi, hwɛ, nda reba a, EWURADZE na ɔse, mebɛma wɔatse ɔko na esebɔ ndze etsia Rabaa a ɔyɛ Ammonmba dze no; na ɔbɛdan amamfo isiw, na wɔdze ogya ahyew ne mbabaa; nna Israel bɛpam hɔn a wɔpaam no no, EWURADZE na ɔse.
3. Hesbon e, bɔ mbubuw, na Ai asɛɛ! Rabaa mbabaa, hom nkeka mu, hom mfura eyitam: hom ntwa sukwadwom, na hom ndzi akɔnaaba wɔ mban mu; na Milkɔm bɔkɔ ndɔmmum, n'asɔfoe na n'asafohemfo nyina.
4. Ɔbabaa ekyirsannyi, ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na ehyehyɛ woho wɔ w'ahoɔdzen mu, w'ahoɔdzen a ɔrokɔ famu no mu? Ɔwo a edze wo werɛ hyɛɛ w'egyapadze mu, dɛ, Woana bɛba mo do?
5. Hwɛ, medze hu fi hɔn a woetwa wo ho ehyia nyina nkyɛn mebɛba wo do, EWURADZE, dɔm EWURADZE na ɔse; na wɔbɔbɔ hom apetse, hom mu nyimpa biara akɔ n'enyim, a obiara nnkɔboaboa eguamfo no ano.
6. Na n'ekyir no medze Ammonmba no befi ndɔmmum asan aba, EWURADZE na ɔse.
7. Edom dze. Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE se nye yi: Aso nyansa nnyi Teman bio? Aso apam ahera abadwembafo? Aso hɔn nyansaa etu ayew?, #Isa 34.5-17; 63.1-6; Eze 25.12-14; 35.1-15; Amos 1.11
8. Hom nguan, hom nsan ekyir, hom ntsena mbrɛ ɔdɔ, Ao Dedanfo! Na medze Esau no mbusu mebɛba no do ber a medze n'asotwe bɛba no do no!
9. Sɛ wenyin abatsewfo mpo na wɔbaa wo do a, aso nkyɛ wonnkegya wenyinaba mpɛpɛw bi? Sɛ ewifo baa anadwe a, nkyɛ hɔn mpo wɔnnkɛsɛɛ ara ekodu dza ɔbɔso hɔn?
10. Naaso emi dze, mama Esau no ho ada hɔ, mama no sumabea ada edzi; na orunntum nnsuma noho. N'asefo asɛɛ, na no nuanom, na n'efisamenafo, na onnyi hɔ.
11. Dan wo ngyanka mba no gya, mobɔkora hɔn do enyikan; na ma w'ekunafo mfa hɔn werɛ ntwer me.
12. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Hwɛ, sɛ hɔn a wɔmmfata dɛ wɔbɔnom kɔɔpow no mu no mpo wɔbɔnom ara ampa a; nna aso ɔwo na ebɛfa woho edzi sɔnn? Ennkɛfa woho edzi sɔnn, na ɔnom ara na ebɔnom.
13. Na maka moho ntam, EWURADZE na ɔse, dɛ Bozra bɛdan ahobowdze, atwetwesidze, amamfo, na ndom, na no nkurow nyinara bɛyɛ amamfo daa.
14. Matse amandzɛɛ bi wɔ EWURADZE nkyɛn, na wɔasoma ahembɔfo wɔ amanaman mu, dɛ, Hom mboa hom ano, na hom mbra no do, na hom nsoɛr mbra akono.
15. Na, hwɛ, mebɛyɛ wo amanaman mu aketseaba, na adasa mu nyia woebu no enyimtsia.
16. Na w'etsiɔdzendze, w'akoma ne ntsɛn adaadaa wo, ɔwo a etse ɔbotan ne mpaapaae mu, ɔwo a akoko a ɔkrɔn kitsa wo nsamu: kaansa eyɛ wo buw wɔ ɔsorsor dɛ ɔkɔr mpo a, medze wo befi hɔ esi famu, EWURADZE na ɔse.
17. Na Edom bɛdan ahobowdze: obiara a otwa mu wɔ ho no no ho bɔbow no, na ɔabɔ no mu ayardɔm nyina ho nhwiroma.
18. Dɛ mbrɛ Sodom na Gomora na nkurow a wɔdeda ho no hɔn mbutuwii tse no, EWURADZE na ɔse, dasanyi biara renntsena hɔ, eso ɔdasanyi ne ba biara rennyɛ ɔmamforanyi wɔ hɔ., #Gye 19.24
19. Hwɛ, ɔbɔfow aba dɛ gyata fi Jordan ne ntsɛn no mu aba tsenabea a ɔyɛ dzen no do: na mebɛma oefi ne nkyɛn eguan awerɛfir mu; na obiara a wɔsan mu yi no no, ɔnoara na medze no besi no do: na woana na ɔtse dɛ emi? Woana bɛhyɛ me ber? Woana nye oguanhwɛfo a obotum m'enyim gyina?
20. Dɛm ntsi hom ntsie EWURADZE n'apam a ɔrepam wɔ Edom ho; na ne tsirmpɔw a ɔabɔ wɔ Teman atsefo ho: Ampaara, wobotwuw hɔn adze akɔ dɛ nguankuw mu nkakraba mpo; ampaara ɔbɛma hɔn tsenabea ayɛ amamfo aka hɔn ho.
21. Hɔn asehwe ne dede ntsi, asaase no popo; nkekamu heei wɔ hɔ a wɔtse ne nka wɔ Mbɛw Po no ho.
22. Hwɛ, ɔbɔfow aba na oetu dɛ ɔkɔr, na ɔatserɛw ne ntsaban mu wɔ Bozra do: na da no Edom mbarimba akatakyi hɔn akoma bɛyɛ dɛ ɔbaa a ɔroko awoo n'akoma.
23. Damaskɔs dze. Hamat n'enyi ato, na Arpad; osiandɛ wɔatse nsɛmbɔn, suro ekitsa hɔn: po do ayɛ begyabegya; wonntum nntaa dzinn.
24. Damaskɔs ayɛ mberɛw, ɔadan noho ruguan, na ahopopo ekitsa no: ahoguan na awerɛhow ekitsa no, dɛ ɔbaa a ɔroko awoo.
25. Ayɛyi kurow no, m'enyigye kurow no, mbrɛ oesi adan no egya?
26. Dɛm ntsi ne mberantsɛ bɔtotɔ wɔ n'abrɔn no mu, na woetwitwa n'asambarimba nyinara egu wɔ da no mu, dɔm EWURADZE na ɔse.
27. Na mobɔsɔ gya wɔ Damaskɔs fasu no mu, na ɔahyew Ben-hadad n'ahemfi no.
28. Kedar, na Hazor n'ahenman a Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar bɔɔ no no ho dze. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Hom nsoɛr, hom nkɔ Kedar, na hom nkɛsɛɛ bokamba no.
29. Hom mfa hɔn asesee na hɔn nguankuw; hom nsoa hɔn ntwamuatam, na hɔn ndzepa, na hɔn efumpɔnkɔ mma hom ho: na hom ntseatsea mu dɛ, Hu etwa hɛnho nyina ehyia.
30. Ao Hazormba e, hom nguan, hom nkyin nkɔ ekyirekyir, hom nkosuma mbrɛ hɔ dɔ, EWURADZE na ɔse. Osiandɛ Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar akɔ hom tsir do apam na ɔabɔ hom ho tsirmpɔw bi.
31. Hom nsoɛr, hom nsoɛr nkɔ ɔman a hɔn ho adwe hɔn a wɔtse hɔ dwudwoodwo no do, EWURADZE na ɔse; hɔn a wonnyi mbobotsen na adaban a hɔn nko ara na wɔtse no.
32. Na hɔn efumpɔnkɔ bɛyɛ asadze, na hɔn anantwi dodow ayɛ afonam: na mobɔbɔ hɔn a woetwitwa ntakuwa no ma apetse mframa nyina mu; na medze hɔn mbusu befi mbea nyina aba hɔn do, EWURADZE na ɔse.
33. Na Hazor bɛyɛ mpataku tsenabea, amamfo daa: ɔdasanyi biara renntsena hɔ, eso ɔdasanyi ne ba biara rennyɛ ɔhɔho wɔ mu.
34. Iyi nye EWURADZE n'asɛm a ɔbaa nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia hɔ wɔ Elam ho wɔ Judahen Zedekia n'ahendzi ahyɛse no.
35. Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE se nye yi: Hwɛ, mubobubu Elam egyen, hɔn tum ne tsitsir mu.
36. Na medze mframa anan mibefi ɔsor mfɛndzanan maba Elam do, na mabɔ hɔn apetse mframa anan no mu nyinara; na ɔman biara nnyi hɔ a Elam tokyemfo no wonnkodu hɔ.
37. Na mebɛma Elam hɔn akoma etu hɔn atamfo, na hɔn a wɔrohwehwɛ hɔn nkwa no enyim: na medze mbusu mebɛba hɔn do, mekyerɛ m'ebufuw hyeehyew no a, EWURADZE na ɔse; na mebɛma afona etsiw hɔn ekodu dɛ mewie hɔn sa:
38. na medze m'ahengua mibesi Elam, na masɛɛ ɔhen na mbapɔmba mefi hɔ, EWURADZE na ɔse.
39. Na ɔbɛba dɛ nda a odzi ekyir no mu no, medze Elam befi ndɔmmum asan aba, EWURADZE na ɔse.

## Tsir 50

1. Asɛm a EWURADZE nam nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia do kaa tsiaa Babilɔn wɔ Kaldeafo asaase ho no.
2. Hom mpaa mu nka wɔ amanaman mu na hom mfa ntahye, na hom nsi frankaa; hom mfa ntahye, na mma hom nnsiw do: hom nse dɛ, Wɔafa Babilɔn, woegu Bel n'enyim ase, Merodak no bo etu; woegu n'ehonyi enyim ase, n'abosom akoma etutu.
3. Na ɔman bi fii kwaamu afamu rutu no do ɔsa a wɔbɛma n'asaase ayɛ amamfo, na obiara renntsena do: woeguanguan, wɔkɔ, nyimpa na mbowa nyina.
4. Nda no mu na aber no mu, EWURADZE na ɔse, Israelmba bɛba, hɔn na Judamba nyina; wɔdze osu botu hɔn kwan wɔakɔhwehwɛ EWURADZE hɔn Nyankopɔn.
5. Wɔbɛdan hɔn enyim akyerɛ Zion do, woebisa ekyir kwan, dɛ, Hom mbra mfa homho mbɔbɔ EWURADZE ho, wɔ daa ahyɛmudzi a werɛ rimmfir no mu.
6. Me man ayɛ nguan a wɔayew: hɔn nguanhwɛfo ama wɔatotɔ gon, na wɔama wɔafomfom kwan wɔ mbepɔw no do: woefi bepɔw do kɔ koko do, hɔn werɛ efir hɔn ahomgyebea.
7. Hɔn a wɔtoo hɔn nyina amemen hɔn: na hɔn atamfo see dɛ, Yɛmmfom, osiandɛ wɔayɛ bɔn etsia EWURADZE, pɛrpɛr tsenabea, mekyerɛ EWURADZE, hɔn egyanom enyidado no.
8. Hom nguan mfi Babilɔn finimfin, na hom mfir edzi mfi Kaldeafo asaase do nkɔ, na hom nyɛ dɛ mpɔnkyenyin a wodzi nguankuw enyim.
9. Na, hwɛ, mibekenyan amanaman akɛse mboanofo ma wofi kwaamu afamu asaase do aba Babilɔn do; na wobotwa no ho mpasuar; na nkyii wɔbɛfa kurow no: hɔn egyen menaba tse dɛ ɔbarimba katakyi nedze; no mu biara nnsan ekyir kwa.
10. Na Kaldea bɛyɛ afonam: hɔn a wɔfa no afo nyinara bɛmee, EWURADZE na ɔse.
11. Hom a hom foom m'egyapadze fae, kaansa hom enyi agye, na hom ridzi ehurusi, kaansa hom adodɔ seradze dɛ nantwifɔr a ɔroporow eburow, na hom su dɛ mpɔnkɔ abran mpo a;
12. hom na n'enyi bɔto papaara; nyia ɔwoo hom no n'enyim bogu ase. Hwɛ, ɔbɛyɛ amanaman mu ekyirkafo, sar, asaase kɛsɛɛ, na sar pradada.
13. Osian EWURADZE n'ebufuw ntsi wɔrenntsena do, na ɔbɛyɛ amamfo koraa: obiara a otwa mu wɔ Babilɔn no no ho bɔbow no, na ɔabɔ nhwiroma wɔ n'amandzehu nyinara ntsi.
14. Hom a hom kontom egyen nyinara, hom mbaa mpasuar ntwa nhyia Babilɔn ho; hom ntotow mbobɔ no, mma hom nnkam hom egyen menaba do: na ɔayɛ bɔn etsia EWURADZE.
15. Hom mbɔ ose ngu no do ntwa nhyia; ɔdze noho ama; n'aban ahwehwe ase, n'afasu edwuruw; na EWURADZE n'awerdzi nye no; hom ndzi no wer; dɛ mbrɛ ɔayɛ no, hom so nyɛ no bi.
16. Hom ntwa duafo no mfi Babilɔn, na nyia osuo kantankrankye no mu wɔ twaber mu no: ahyɛdo afona no ho suro ntsi, hɔn mu biara bɛdan noho akɔ no nkorɔfo hɔ, na hɔn mu obiara eguan akɔ nankasa n'asaase do.
17. Israel yɛ nguantsen a wɔabɔ apetse; ngyata no apam no kɔ; asɔpɔn no Asiriahen bɛtsetseew no mu; na ekyirii Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar yi bobubuu ne mbiew mu.
18. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE Israel Nyankopɔn no se nye yi: Hwɛ, mebɛtsea Babilɔnhen na n'asaase, dɛ mbrɛ matsea Asiriahen yi.
19. Na medze Israel bɛsan aba n'edzidzibea, na oedzidzi wɔ Karmel na Basan, na ne kra amee wɔ Efraim akoko do na Gilead.
20. Nda no mu, na aber no mu, EWURADZE na ɔse, wɔbɔhwehwɛ Israel emumuyɛ ekyir kwan, na worinnya bi; na Juda no bɔn so, na wonnkohu: na medze befir hɔn a mebɛdan hɔn megya dɛ nkaasefo no.
21. Tu Merataim asaase no do sa, ɔnoara no do a, na Pekod atsefo no do: kuku na sɛɛ nkaasefo no korakora, EWURADZE na ɔse, na yɛ dɛ mbrɛ mahyɛ wo nyinara.
22. Ɔko ne dede gyegye asaase no do, na ɔsɛɛ kɛse so dze.
23. Mbrɛ woetwitwa na woebubu asaase nyina hamɛr no mu esinesin a! Mbrɛ Babilɔn edua adan amamfo wɔ amanaman mu a!
24. Babilɔn, mesua wo efir na wɔapa wo so, na ɔwoara ennhu: woehu wo, na wɔakyer wo so, osiandɛ enye EWURADZE edzi aperper.
25. EWURADZE ebua n'akoradze dan na woeyi n'ebufuhyew akodze epue: osiandɛ EWURADZE, dɔm EWURADZE no, wɔ dwuma bi dzi wɔ Kaldeafo asaase do.
26. Hom mfir mfɛndzanan mbra no do, hom mbuebue n'eburosan no: hom ntutu no ngu dɛ efiefi, na hom nsɛɛ no huntuhuntu: mma hom mma no mu biribi nnka.
27. Hom nkuku n'anantwinyin nyina; hom mma wɔnsan nkɔ ekumii. Wondue! Osiandɛ hɔn da edu, hɔn asotweber no a.
28. Hom ntsie hɔn a woguan na wofi nsa fi Babilɔn asaase do, dɛ wɔrekɛpaa mu aka EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn n'awerdzi, n'asɔrfi ho awerdzi akyerɛ no hɔn ndze.
29. Hom mfrɛ egyentofo no nyinara nkɔtoatoa Babilɔn, hɔn a wɔkontom egyen no nyinara; hom mbɔ nseraban ntwa no ho nhyia; mma hom mma no mu obiara mmfi nsa: hom nsusu n'edwuma do nhyɛ no ananmu; dɛ mbrɛ ɔno ɔayɛ nyinara no, hom so nyɛ no bi: osiandɛ ɔayɛ EWURADZE no do nkontompɔ, Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi no do a.
30. Dɛm ntsi na ne mberantsɛ bɔtotɔ n'abrɔn do, na wɔbɛma ne mbarimba akofo nyinara wɔayɛ foo wɔ da no mu, EWURADZE na ɔse.
31. Hwɛ, ɔwo ɔkontompɔnyi, menye wo enya, EWURADZE, dɔm Ewuradze no na ɔse: osiandɛ wo da no edu, ber a medze bɔtwe w'aso no a.
32. Na ɔkontompɔnyi no befintsiw na ɔahwe ase, na obiara remma no do: na mubokua gya wɔ no kurow no mu, na ɔahyew dza abɔ no ho aprɔw nyinara.
33. Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE se nye yi: wɔatseetsee Israelmba na Juda prɛko: na hɔn a wɔfaa hɔn ndɔmmum nyina dzedze hɔn mu dzen; wɔpow dɛ wɔbɛma wɔakɔ.
34. Hɔn pomfo yɛ dzen; ne dzin dze dɔm EWURADZE: obedzi hɔn asɛm kofekofe ama hɔn, na ɔama asaase no ahomgye, na ɔahyɛ Babilɔnfo no ahomtsew.
35. Afona wɔ Kaldeafo do, EWURADZE na ɔse, na Babilɔnfo no do, na n'asafohen na n'enyansafo no do.
36. Afona wɔ ahohyehyɛfo no do, na wɔbɛyɛ akwasampafo! Afona wɔ hɔn mbarimba akatakyi no do, na hɔn akoma botutu.
37. Afona wɔ hɔn mpɔnkɔ na hɔn ntseaseanam do, na aforaforafo a wɔwɔ no mu no nyina do, ama wɔaayɛ dɛ mbaa: afona wɔ n'akoradze do, ama woeewia.
38. Weseeyɛ wɔ n'esu do, na wɔbɔwewew: osiandɛ ɔyɛ ehonyi a woesian asaase, na wɔabobɔ adam wɔ abosom ho.
39. Dɛm ntsi sar do mbowa abɔyafo wɔnye mpataku bɛtsena wɔ hɔ, na nsohor bɛtsena mu: na wɔrenntsena do bio dabiarada; eso wɔrenntsena do bio ofi ebusuasantsen kɛpem ebusuasantsen.
40. Dɛ mbrɛ Nyankopɔn butuuw Sodom na Gomora na hɔn ho nkurow no, EWURADZE na ɔse; dɛmara so na nyimpa biara renntsena hɔ, eso nyimpa biara rennyɛ ɔmamforanyi wɔ hɔ.
41. Hwɛ, ɔman bi fi kwaamu afamu reba; na wobekenyan ɔman kɛse, na ahemfo pii efi asaase ne mfɛndzanan noho.
42. Wokurakura egyen na peaa; hɔn tsir yɛ dzen, na wonnyi ehumbɔbɔr; hɔn ndze wor dɛ po, na wɔtsetse mpɔnkɔ do; obiara etwa mpasuar, dɛ ɔbarimba a ɔrokɔ akono wɔ wo do, Ao Babilɔn babaa!
43. Babilɔnhen atse hɔn nka, na n'abaw egura: nketsenketse akyer no, na yaw a ɔtse dɛ ɔbaa a ɔwɔ awoko mu.
44. Hwɛ, ɔbɔfow dɛ gyata fi Jordan ne ntsɛn no mu abɛtsena bea a ɔyɛ dzen no do, na mebɛma woeguan efi me nkyɛn awerɛfir mu; na obiara a wɔasan mu eyi no no, ɔno na medze no besi no do: na woana na ɔtse dɛ emi? Woana na ɔbɛhyɛ me mber? Woana nye oguanhwɛfo no a obegyina m'enyim no?
45. Dɛm ntsi hom ntsie EWURADZE n'apam a ɔapam etsia Babilɔn no; na ne tsirmpɔw a ɔabɔ etsia Kaldeafo asaase no: Ampaara wobotwuw hɔn adze akɔ, mekyerɛ nguankuw mu nkakraba no; ampaara ɔbɛma hɔn tsenabea ayɛ amamfo ama hɔn.
46. Babilɔn ne gye ne dede ntsi, asaase wosow, na wɔtse nkekamu no wɔ amanaman mu.

## Tsir 51

1. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Hwɛ, mobɔbɔ ɔsɛɛ mframa aba Babilɔn do, na hɔn a wɔtse Leb-kamai do.
2. Na mobɔsoma ahɔho akɔ Babilɔn, na woekohuw no. Wɔbɔto n'asaase no pan: na ɔfona da no mu wobotwa no ho ehyia etsia no.
3. Mma egyentonyi no nnkontom n'egyen, na mma ɔmmema noho do wɔ ne dadzetar no mu: na mma hom nngyaa ne mberantsɛ no; hom nsɛɛ no dɔm nyinara huntuhuntu.
4. Na wɔbɔtotɔ ahwehwe ase wɔ Kaldeafo asaase do, na woeehwirahwira hɔn mu wɔ n'abrɔn mu.
5. Na Israel anaa Juda hɔn Nyankopɔn, dɔm EWURADZE no, ɔnndaan hɔn nngyaae; kaansa afɔdzi ahyɛ hɔn asaase do ma etsia Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi no mpo a.
6. Hom nguan mfi Babilɔn mu, na nyimpa biara ngye noho nkwa; mma wonntwa hom nkyen wɔ n'emumuyɛ mu; na EWURADZE n'awerdziber nye no; obotua no n'ahyɛnanmu kaw no.
7. Nna Babilɔn yɛ sika kɔɔpow wɔ EWURADZE nsamu a ɔmaa asaase nyinara bowee: amanaman anom ne nsa bi; dɛm ntsi na amanaman abobɔ adam.
8. Babilɔn ahwe ase awerɛfir mu asɛɛ: hom ntwa ewuo mma no; hom mfa ne yaw n'ano edur mbra, bi a wɔsa no yarba a ɔbɛyɛ yie.
9. Nkyɛ yɛresa Babilɔn yarba, naaso annsa. Hom ndan no ngya, na hom mma hɛn mu biara nkɔ nankasa no kurow mu: osiandɛ n'atsɛmbu edu ɔsor, na wɔama do ekodu wimu wimu mpo.
10. EWURADZE eyi hɛn tsenenee edzi: hom mbra, ma yɛnkɛka EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn n'edwuma nkyerɛ wɔ Zion.
11. Hom nsew egyen menaba no ano; hom nsuo akokyɛm no mu dzen: EWURADZE ekenyan Media ahemfo hɔn sunsum; osiandɛ wɔabɔ Babilɔn ho tsirmpɔw dɛ ɔbɛsɛɛ no: na EWURADZE n'awerdzi, n'asɔrfi ho awerdzi nye no.
12. Hom nsi frankaa ntsia Babilɔn afasu, hom mma aweɔn mu nyɛ dzen, hom mfa aweɔmfo nsisi, hom nsiesie atsɛwfo: na EWURADZE ahyehyɛ wɔ ne tsirmu, na eso ɔayɛ dza ɔkae wɔ Babilɔnfo ho no.
13. Ao ɔwo a etse esu pii do, w'akoradze dɔɔ so, w'ewiei aba, w'enyikaber esusudze no a.
14. Dɔm EWURADZE aka noho ntam, dɛ, Ampaara medze nyimpa mebɛhyɛ wo ma, dɛ mbɛbɛw; na wɔabɔ wo do ose.
15. Ɔno na ɔdze no tum ayɛ asaase, ɔno na ɔdze ne nyansaa etsintsim wiadze, na ɔdze ne ntseasee atserɛw ɔsorsor mu.
16. Sɛ ɔbɔ ne ndze mu a, esu no weɔɔyɛ ba ɔsorsor, na ɔma ehubɔhubɔw tu fi asaase ano fa sor; ɔno na ɔyɛ enyinam na nyankom, na ɔdze mframa fi n'adzekorabea ba.
17. Nyimpa biara abɛyɛ dɛ abowa na onnyim dze; osikadwinnyi biara ne sianhonyi hyɛ no enyito: na no guhonyi yɛ ator, na ahom biara nnyi hɔn mu.
18. Wɔyɛ egyangyandze, ndaadaa dwuma a: hɔn asotweber mu wɔbɛhera.
19. Jakob ne kyɛfa nntse dɛ iyinom; na ɔno nye adze nyinara ne yɛfo; na Israel nye n'egyapadze ebusuakuw; dɔm EWURADZE nye ne dzin.
20. Ɔwo nye m'ekuma na m'akondadze; ɔwo na medze mubobubu amanaman mu esinesin; na medze ɔwo mebɛsɛɛ ahendzi;
21. na medze ɔwo mubobubu pɔnkɔ na nyia ɔtse no do no mu esinesin;
22. na medze ɔwo mubobubu tseaseanam na nyia ɔtse mu no mu esinesin; na medze ɔwo mubobubu ɔbanyin na ɔbaa mu esinesin; na medze ɔwo mubobubu akɔdaa na abofra mu esinesin; na medze ɔwo mubobubu aberantsɛ na ababaawa no mu esinesin;
23. na medze ɔwo mubobubu oguanhwɛfo na no nguankuw no mu esinesin; na medze ɔwo mubobubu ɔnantwi na ne mpamho no mu esinesin; na medze ɔwo mubobubu ambradofo na amampanyin no mu esinesin.
24. Na mubotua Babilɔn na Kaldeafo no nyinara kaw wɔ hɔn mbusu a wɔabɔ no hom enyim wɔ Zion no nyinara ho, EWURADZE na ɔse.
25. Hwɛ, menye wo enya, bepɔw sɛɛfo, EWURADZE na ɔse, ɔwo esɛɛ asaase nyinara: na mebɛtsen me nsa wɔ wo do, na mepirepirew wo mefi abotan no do, na mayɛ wo bepɔw hyewee.
26. Na wɔremmfa wo mu ɔbo bi nnto kutuwdo, anaa ɔbo bi nnto fapem; na ebɛyɛ amamfo daa, EWURADZE na ɔse.
27. Hom nsi frankaa wɔ asaase no do, hom nhɛn akasamu no wɔ amanaman mu, hom nsiesie amanaman nkyer no ho sa, hom nhyia Ararat, Minni, na Askenaz ahendzi nyinara mbra no do; hom nhyɛ ɔsahen mbra no do; hom mfa mpɔnkɔ mbra dɛ mbɛbɛw wirikyee.
28. Hom nsiesie amanaman ntu no do ɔsa, Media ahemfo hɔn ambradofo, na hɔn amampanyin nyinara, na no tumdzi asaase no nyinara.
29. Na asaase no ho popo na ɔtseetsee: osiandɛ EWURADZE ne tsirmpɔw a ɔwɔ Babilɔn do no osi pi, dɛ ɔbɛyɛ Babilɔn amamfo a obiara nnyi mu.
30. Babilɔn akatakyi no woegyaa ko, wɔaka hɔn akoban no mu; hɔn ahoɔdzen apa; wɔayɛ dɛ mbasiafo; wɔato ne tsenabea mu ogya; woebubu n'adaban mu.
31. Mbirikatufo baako botu mbirika ekehyia ɔbaako so, na ɔbɔfo baako ekehyia ɔbaako so akɔbɔ amandzɛɛ akyerɛ Babilɔnhen dɛ wɔagye no kurow no wɔ mbea nyinara:
32. na wɔagye etwae no, na wɔdze ogya ahyew ndzɛmbir no, na mbarimba akofo no bo etutu.
33. Na mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no se nye yi: Babilɔn babaa tse dɛ ewuporoweebea ber a wotsiatsia do no; aka mber kakra, ma twaber edu ama no.
34. Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar awe me, ɔadwerew me, ɔayɛ me dɛ kyɛnse pan, ɔamen me dɛ nsu mu abowapɔn ɔdze m'akɔndɔdze ahyɛ ne yafun ma; oepuw me egu.
35. Nyia a ɔtse Zion bɛka dɛ, Etsirmɔdzendze a wɔdze ayɛ emi na mo honam no ɔmbra Babilɔn do; na Jerusalɛm bɛka dɛ, Mo bɔgyaa ngu Kaldeafo do.
36. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Hwɛ, mibedzi w'asɛm ama wo, na medzi wer ama wo; na mobɔwew no po, na mama no nsunyiwa ayɛ wesee.
37. Na Babilɔn bɛdan amamfo, mpataku tsenabea, ahobowdze, na asesardze a obiara nntse mu.
38. Hɔn nyinara bɔbobɔ mu awor dɛ ngyatafɔr; wɔbɔpɔw dɛ ngyatamba.
39. Sɛ hɔn ho hyehye hɔn a, mobɔto hɔn pon, na mama wɔabobow, na woedzi ehurusi, na wɔada daa nda prɛko, na wonnkenyan, EWURADZE na ɔse.
40. Medze hɔn besian dɛ nguambaa akɔ ekumii, dɛ nguannyin ɔnye mpɔnkyenyin.
41. Mbrɛ woedua agye Sesak  a! Mbrɛ asaase nyina ayɛyi no wɔafa no mprase a! Mbrɛ Babilɔn edua adan amamfo wɔ amanaman mu a!
42. Po abɛseram Babilɔn do: n'asorɛkye dodow akɛtaa no do.
43. No nkurow adan afo, asaase kɛsɛɛ, na sar, asaase a ɔdasanyi biara nntsena do, eso nyimpa ne ba biara nntwa mu wɔ hɔ.
44. Na mubobu atsɛn megu Bel do wɔ Babilɔn, na meyi dza ɔamemen no mefi n'anomu epue; na amanaman nnkɔbɔ mu apem akɔ ne nkyɛn ara bio: nyew, Babilɔn ɔfasu ahwe ase!
45. Me man, hom mfi no mu mfir, na hom mu nyimpa biara ngye noho mfi EWURADZE n'ebufuhyew mu.
46. Eso mma hom akoma nntu, eso mma hom nnsuro wɔ akwansosɛm a hom bɛtse wɔ asaase no do no ho; na akwansosɛm kor bɛba afe kor mu, na n'ekyir afe kor so mu akwansosɛm, na akatabansɛm aba asaase no do, nyia odzi tum oetsia nyia odzi tum.
47. Dɛm ntsi, hwɛ, nda reba a mubobubu atsɛn egu Babilɔn sianhonyi do, na n'asaase no nyina n'enyi bɔto; na n'atɔfoe nyina bɔhwehwe ase wɔ ne finimfin.
48. Nna enyigye ntsi ɔsor na asaase, na dza ɔwɔ mu nyinara bɔtow Babilɔn ho ndwom; na afofafo befi kwaamu afamu aba no do, EWURADZE na ɔse.
49. Dɛ mbrɛ Babilɔn maa Israel atɔfo hwehwee ase no, dɛmara so Babilɔn na asaase nyina hɔn atɔfoe bɔhwehwe ase wɔ hɔ.
50. Hom a hom efi afona anomu, hom nduom, na mma hom nngyina komm; hom mfi ekyirekyir nkaa EWURADZE, na hom mma Jerusalɛm mbra hom adwen mu.
51. Hɛn enyi ato, osiandɛ yɛatse ahorbahyɛ nka; enyimguase akata hɛn enyim: osiandɛ ananaben aba EWURADZE ne fie krɔnkrɔnmbea no do.
52. Ɔno ntsi, hwɛ, nda reba a, EWURADZE na ɔse, mubobu ne sianhonyi nyina atsɛn; na epirafo besi nkrum wɔ n'asaase nyina do.
53. Sɛ Babilɔn fow kɔ sor mpo, na ɔkyekyer n'ahoɔdzen sorɔnsorɔmbea no akoban mpo a me nkyɛn ara na afofafo befir aba no do, EWURADZE na ɔse.
54. Nkekamu a ofi Babilɔn, na ɔsɛɛ kɛse a ofi Kaldeafo asaase do ne ndze na ɔda mu no!
55. Osiandɛ EWURADZE refa Babilɔn afo, na ɔma no mu ndze kɛse no sɛɛ fi mu; na hɔn asorɛkye wor dɛ esu pii na hɔn ndze gyegye huoo:
56. na afofanyi no aba no do, Babilɔn do a, na wɔafa ne mbarimba akatakyi no, woebubu hɔn ngyen mu esinesin: na EWURADZE yɛ ahyɛnanmu Nyankopɔn, tua ara na obotua hɔn kaw.
57. Na mebɛma n'asafohen na n'enyansafo, n'ambradofo na n'amampanyin na n'akatakyi no wɔabobow; na wɔbɛda daa nda prɛko, na wonnkenyan, Ɔhen a ne dzin dze dɔm EWURADZE no na ɔse.
58. Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE se nye yi: Babilɔn afasu atɛtɛr no, wobodwuruw no pasaa, na wɔdze ogya ahyew no mbobotsen atsentsen no; na ɔman no bɛberɛ ama egyangyandze, na amanaman no aberɛ ama ogya; na wɔbɔtɔ bahaw.
59. Asɛm a nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia dze hyɛɛ Maseia ba Neria ne ba Seraia, ber a ɔnye Judahen Zedekia kɔr Babilɔn wɔ n'ahendzi afe a otsia anan no mu nye yi. Afei na Seraia yɛ gyaasehen.
60. Na Jeremia kyerɛɛw mbusu a ɔbɛba Babilɔn do nyina hyɛɛ nwoma mu, mekyerɛ nsɛm a wɔakyerɛw no wɔ Babilɔn ho yi nyina.
61. Na Jeremia see Seraia, dɛ, Sɛ idu Babilɔn a, ɔno hwɛ na kenkan nsɛm yi nyina,
JER.51.62, na se dɛ, EWURADZE, ɔwo na akasa bea yi ho dɛ ibotwa no akyen, amma obiara aanntsena mu, nyimpa o, abowa o, na mbom dɛ ɔnyɛ amamfo ara daa.
63. Na ɔmbra dɛ sɛ iwie nwoma yi kenkan a, fa ɔbo kyekyer ho, na tow kyen Eufrates mu:
64. na ka dɛ, Dɛm na Babilɔn bɔdɔ, na onnkopue bio wɔ mbusu a medze mebɛba do no ntsi: na wɔbɔtɔ bahaw. Mbrɛ Jeremia nsɛm yi pem nye ha.

## Tsir 52

1. Zedekia bedzii hen no nna oedzi mfe eduonu biako; na odzii hen mfe dubiako wɔ Jerusalɛm: na ne na dzin dze Hamutal, Jeremia a ofi Libna ne babaa a.
2. Na ɔyɛɛ dza omuo wɔ EWURADZE enyiwa do, dɛ mbrɛ Jehoiakim yɛe no nyinara.
3. Na ɔnam EWURADZE n'ebufuw do na ɔbaa dɛm wɔ Jerusalɛm na Juda, dze bodur dɛ ɔtoow hɔn fii n'enyim kyenee: na Zedekia tseew Babilɔnhen no do etua.
4. Na ɔbaa dɛ n'ahendzi afe a otsia akron no mu no, bosoom a otsia du no, nna Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar botuaa Jerusalɛm, ɔno na no dɔm nyinara, na wɔkyeer do nsera; na wɔtoow aban bɔɔ ho aprɔw tsiaa no.
5. Nna wotuaa kurow no kodur ɔhen Zedekia n'afe a otsia dubiako no.
6. Bosoom a otsia anan no mu, bosoom no ne nda akron no mu no, ɔkɔm yɛɛ dzendzenndzen wɔ kurow no mu ara, ma wonnyaa edziban biara mma asaase no do nkorɔfo no.
7. Nna wotuetuee kurow no ho, na mbarimba akofo no nyina guanguanee fii kurow no mu anadwe dze faa afasu ebien no ntamu, abobow kɛse no a ɔwɔ ɔhen no ture no ho no kɔree; (afei na Kaldeafo etwa kurow no ho ehyia:) na wɔdze faa Araba kwan no do kɔree.
8. Na Kaldeafo dɔm no tsiiw ɔhen no, na wɔkɔtoo Zedekia wɔ Jeriko tɛtɛr mu; na no dɔm nyina fii ne nkyɛn petsee.
9. Nna wɔkyeer ɔhen no, na wɔdze no kɛmaa Babilɔnhen wɔ Ribla a ɔwɔ Hamat asaase do no; na obuaa no atsɛn.
10. Na Babilɔnhen kum Zedekia ne mbabanyin no wɔ n'enyim: okunkum Juda asafohen nyinara so wɔ Ribla.
11. Na otutuu Zedekia n'enyiwa; na Babilɔnhen dze no too mpokyerɛ mu, na ɔdze no kɔr Babilɔn, na ɔdze no too efiadze kodur dɛ owui.
12. Afei bosoom a otsia enum no mu no, bosoom no ne dadu a ɔyɛ ɔhen Nebukadenezar, Babilɔnhen no n'afe a otsia duakron no mu no, aweɔmfo safohen Nebuzaradan a ogyina Babilɔnhen no n'enyim no, ɔbaa Jerusalɛm:
13. na ɔhyeew EWURADZE ne fi na ɔhen no ne fi; na Jerusalɛm efi nyinara, ofi kɛse biara mpo na ɔdze ogya hyeew no.
14. Na Kaldeafo dɔm a wɔka aweɔmfo safohen no ho nyinara dwuruuw Jerusalɛm afasu no nyina hyiae.
15. Nna aweɔmfo safohen Nebuzaradan soaa ɔman no mu ehiafo neminemi no bi kɔr ndɔmmum, na ɔman no mu nkaa a wɔkaa kurow no mu, na awaefo a wɔwaae kɔr Babilɔnhen nkyɛn na nyimpadodow no mu nkaa no.
16. Na aweɔmfo safohen Nebuzaradan daan asaase no mu ehiafo neminemi no bi gyae dɛ wɔnyɛ wenyin tureahwɛfo na ekuafo.
17. Na boran edum no a ɔwɔ EWURADZE fie no, na ngyinado na boran po a ɔwɔ EWURADZE fie no, Kaldeafo no bubuu mu esinesin, na wɔsoaa boran a ɔwɔ ho no nyina kɔr Babilɔn.
18. Nsenaba so, na nsofi, na edumgya, na mbɛɛsen, na ntser, na boran nkɔɔpow a wɔdze som nyina, wɔfae kɔree.
19. Na nkɔɔpow, na ogya asɛn, na mbɛɛsen, na nsenaba, na nkandzeadua, na ntser, na nkɔɔpow; dza ɔyɛ sika dze no, wɔ sika mu, dza ɔyɛ dwetɛ dze no, wɔ dwetɛ mu, na aweɔmfo safohen no fae kɔree.
20. Edum ebien, po kor no, na boran anantwi duebien a ɔwɔ ngyinado no a ɔhen Solomon yɛe maa EWURADZE fi no n'ase no: nkɔɔpow yinom nyinara no boran no woenntum ennker.
21. Na ɔyɛ edum no dze, nkyindur ndua kor no krɔn yɛ basafa akron; na ahoma basafa esia twa ho hyia; na ne peperepee nsatseaba anan: na tu da mu.
22. Na ne tsir no boran a; na tsir kor no krɔn yɛ basafa ebien na fa, na atena na pɔmegranate eduaba wɔ tsir no ho hyia, ne nyinara boran a: na nkyindur ndua a otsia ebien no, no ho wɔ dɛmara bi, na pɔmegranate eduaba so.
23. Na pɔmegranate ekutu eduokron esia wɔ afa na afa; na pɔmegranate ekutu a ɔwɔ atena no ho hyia nyina yɛ ɔha.
24. Na aweɔmfo safohen no faa ɔsɔfopanyin Seraia, na ɔsɔfo edziekyir Zefania, na abowanoahwɛfo baasa:
25. na kurow no mu na ɔfaa ɔpanyin a wɔdze no sii mbarimba akofo no do; na hɔn a wohun ɔhen no enyim, beesuon a wohun hɔn wɔ kurow no mu no; na ɔsahen ne kyerɛwnyi a ɔpon asaase no do nkorɔfo kɔ ɔsa; na asaase no do nkorɔfo no mu mbarimba eduosia a wohun hɔn kurow no mu no.
26. Na aweɔmfo safohen Nebuzaradan faa hɔn, dze hɔn kɛmaa Babilɔnhen wɔ Ribla.
27. Na Babilɔnhen bobɔɔ hɔn, na okunkum hɔn wɔ Ribla a ɔwɔ Hamat asaase do no do. Dɛm na wɔfaa Juda ndɔmmum fii n'asaase do kɔree.
28. Nkorɔfo a Nebukadenezar soaa hɔn ndɔmmum kɔree no nye woyinom: afe a otsia esuon no mu Judafo mpensa eduonu ebiasa:
29. Nebukadenezar n'afe a otsia duawɔtwe no mu no ɔsoaa nyimpa ahaawɔtwe eduasa ebien ndɔmmum fii Jerusalɛm:
30. Nebukadenezar n'afe a otsia eduonu ebiasa no mu na aweɔmfo safohen Nebuzaradan soaa Judafo ahaesuon eduanan enum ndɔmmum kɔree: nyimpa nyinara wɔyɛ mpemanan ahaesia.
31. Na ɔbaa dɛ Judahen Jehoiakin no ndɔmmumkɔ afe a otsia eduasa esuon no mu, bosoom a otsia duebien no mu, bosoom no ne da a otsia eduonu enum no mu, na Babilɔnhen Evil-merodak, n'ahendzi afe a odzi kan no mu, ɔmaa Judahen Jehoiakin ne tsir do, na oyii no fii efiadze puei;
32. na ɔnye no kasaa kasa pa, na ɔmaa n'akɔngua kyɛɛn ahemfo a wɔnye no wɔ Babilɔn no hɔn akɔngua.
33. Na ɔsesaa n'efiadzenda atar no, na odzidzii wɔ n'enyim daa no nkwa nda nyinara.
34. Na ɔyɛ n'akɔhomabɔdze no, wɔdze ne daa akɔhomabɔdze no maa no fii Babilɔnhen no ne nkyɛn, da biara n'afamudze wɔ no nkwa nda nyinara mu, dze kodur no wu da.
